DEIERTED MILL

Having nightly increased in attraction, and many of its peculiar and interesting
situations having elicited from crowded audiences such spontaneous and fervent
applause as has rarely been witnessed within the walls of any Theatre, t h e
Manager would not feel himself justified in entirely withdrawing it from representation—but having pledged himself to the revival of the Romantic Fairy Tale of

Till!

FOMTY

THIBYES!

it is respectfully announced, that it will be performed as the First Piece on Monday
and Tuesday; and 1 he D E S E R T E D MILL on Wednesday, Thursday, & Friday,
being the Last Night of the Season.

Jericho, St. Petersburg, Van IMeraan's Land, Halifax, and all intermediate places,
to prevent the possibility of any Manager entertaining the slightest idea of
engaging the UNFABAIXELED Mrs, P H Z W l l W a l , until the expected
attraction of THESEUS AND AKIADHE is sufficiently abated,

and Gentlemen, Patrons of the Italian Opera, he will endeavour to produce, with the assistance of
Sis PUZZI, who has undertaken the superintendence of the Stage and Orchestra Departments,

DURING T H E P R E S E N T W I N T E R SEASON,

the Support and Patronage which he respectfully solicits.

T H E T H E A rTRREE has been "ready altered, under the Direction of Mr. BEAZLEY. The whole of the Dress Circle converted into Private Boxes, and a number of Stalls
constructed; the Subscription to which for the Season will be upon moderate Terms.

At the request of many Noblemen, who ham already signified their intention of Patronising this undertaking, the Opera will not commence before Half-past Eight o'Cloek.
